The significant UK label has gained a new logo for its capsule collection, launching this week. The cube-shaped logo, rendered in shades of grey, appears on each piece, including t-shirts, socks, coach jackets and bucket hats. It’s a bold move for the label, which has ‘consciously avoided’ emphasising logos in the past, says co-founder Jimmy Collins.</p> \n<p>But, in a time of forced disconnection, YMC looked to a friendly face to work on the project, as a way of introducing a revitalised energy. Family friend Pref, a British graphic artist working in <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/typography\" title=\"Typography\">typography</a> and graffiti, has been known to the brand since childhood. He used the YMC (You Must Create) wording to inspire the logo’s design.</p> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-287410\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"1\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/000075270009_final.jpg?itok=y8wKxKY3\" width=\"1388\" height=\"1703\" alt=\"\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>‘The unique combination of characters and words in the brand names and slogans gave me an opportunity to create something new with my style,’ he explains. ‘Each varying combination of letters offers different visual possibilities. My final aim is to create something that is technical and innovative but at the same time legible, simple and concise.’</p> \n<p>While 2020 is now known universally as a year of (not so great) surprises, YMC has relievingly provided us with its familiar, punk-ish and London-centric feel throughout the capsule, with the rejuvenated logo marking the biggest shift.</p> \n<p>All involved put the project’s success down to the neighbourly, collaborative tone of the partnership. ‘Working with Pref has been a collision of worlds in many ways,’ says Collins. ‘His work with <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/typography\" title=\"Typography\">typography</a>, strong words and humour was the reason we approached him.’</p> \n<p>Pref agrees: ‘It’s important to curate the right artist/brand with the right style and ethos, more than anything else – once that’s done the rest of process should take care of itself. Each side of the collaboration must compliment the other and feel free to do what it is they do without being hindered. A successful collaboration should make it possible to stretch beyond what might normally be possible for each of the parties on their own.’ §</p>\n<img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~4/e1RKx0hhbvo\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\" />","descriptionType":"text/html","publishedDate":"Thu, 13 Aug 2020 17:01:45 +0000","feedId":9788,"bgimg":"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/wp_large/s3/2020/08/ymcf.jpg","linkMd5":"ebf1c18db6d791c574a1f41e0e202415","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn8@2020_4/2020/08/25/00-35-16-066_f55ae36bf5973aa9.webp","destWidth":484,"destHeight":565,"sourceBytes":28442,"destBytes":18330,"author":"","enclosureType":"image/jpeg","enclosureUrl":"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/wp_large/s3/2020/08/ymcf.jpg","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/000075270009_final.jpg?itok=y8wKxKY3":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn51@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-16-853_44fe4d943b80cede.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~4/e1RKx0hhbvo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn88@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-17-336_99ec5c0b3ab9cec1.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598315696879},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 08:34:56","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:34:56","title":"Designer Norma Kamali’s morning meditation routine","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~3/upbYa8ohbik/designer-norma-kamali-shares-her-morning-meditation-routine","description":"<p>Long before ‘wellness’ made its way into our vocabulary, Norma Kamali was putting <a href=\"https://www.wallpaper.com/tags/wellness\" target=\"_self\">healthy rituals</a> at the heart of her brand. The legendary <a href=\"https://www.wallpaper.com/tags/new-york\" target=\"_self\">New York</a> designer who dressed Studio 54, was an early force in creating what would later be termed ‘athleisure’. With the puffer coat and high heeled sneaker among her other design innovations, she has always been one step ahead.</p>\n<p>Growing up in NYC in the 1950s, Kamali’s mother was an advocate for juicing, encouraging a life-long dedication to plant-based living. The loss of many dear friends to the AIDS virus in the 1980s would intensify her search for natural products and self-care practices.</p>\n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\">\n<div id=\"file-287227\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\">\n<div class=\"content\">\n    <img alt=\"black and white beauty and wellness products owned by Norma Kamali\" title=\"black and white beauty and wellness products owned by Norma Kamali\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"1\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/swf_norma.jpg?itok=88eX96KI\" width=\"667\" height=\"1000\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"image-caption\">\nA peek inside this bathroom cabinet of designer by Norma Kalamli\n</div>\n<p>Today, her 56th street flagship boutique boasts a wellness cafe, and she has recently ventured into skincare with the launch of her lifestyle range, NORMALIFE.</p>\n<p>For Kamali, life is about aging with power, ‘anti-aging’ and ‘anti-wrinkle’ are words we should eliminate from descriptions of aging, she says. ‘You look good for your age is another!’ A good night’s sleep underpins all of her self-care practices. Preparation for sleep begins the minute you wake and everything you do throughout the day affects your sleep, not just when you put your head on the pillow.</p>\n<p>Here, the designer shares with us the seven steps to her healthy morning rituals - from sun salutations to steam showers and green juices.</p>\n<h2>Wake up early</h2>\n<p>I require seven to eight hours sleep a night and therefore I am in bed early to wake up at 5am. My bedroom is dark and the temperature cool and I wake up without an alarm. By waking up early I have time to follow my morning rituals. A good sleep is so important for me as it diffuses the stresses of the day, but I also find that many of my creative ideas come to me in my sleep, or just as I wake.</p>\n<h2>Brush teeth with tooth soap</h2>\n<p>The ingredients from tooth soap [sugar-free tooth cleaning droplets] work as a pulling method to remove bacteria from the mouth. I then use a mouth rinse called Swish that alkalines the body.</p>\n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\">\n<div id=\"file-287229\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\">\n<div class=\"content\">\n    <img alt=\"black and white illustration of woman meditating in leopard spandex and glasses \" title=\"black and white illustration of woman meditating in leopard spandex and glasses \" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"2\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/normalife_body2.jpg?itok=BV_Qhfgj\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1697\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"image-caption\">\n<em>Illustrations by Gian Furlan </em>\n</div>\n<h2>Drink lemon and ginger warm water</h2>\n<p>I use lemon and ginger as a morning tea that is comforting but also helps with the elimination of toxins. The lemon and ginger are digestives and prepare me for a later on break of the fast.</p>\n<h2>Cat cow stretches and sun salutations</h2>\n<p>The energy of the movements for 15 minutes helps the blood flow.</p>\n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\">\n<div id=\"file-287230\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\">\n<div class=\"content\">\n    <img alt=\"black and white illustration of woman doing yoga posses in leopard spandex and glasses \" title=\"black and white illustration of woman doing yoga posses in leopard spandex and glasses \" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"3\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/normalife_body4.jpg?itok=q5q-PmlU\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1697\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"image-caption\">\n<em>Illustrations by Gian Furlan </em>\n</div>\n<h2>Breathing meditation</h2>\n<p>I sit comfortably and let my heart and mind settle into my breath and slow the breath to long slow repetitions. I dedicate my meditation everyday and my mind starts a creative idea process that works best in the morning. I have been practicing meditation since 1970.</p>\n<h2>Steam shower</h2>\n<p>Before I shower I fully do a dry massage with SMOOTH my exfoliant, made with charcoal and aloe and finely ground olive pits all over face and body. As the colour changes from black to a pale shade I enter the shower and rinse my skin to a smooth moisturised finish. I turn on the steam and breath in the moisture. Steam showers are like moisturisers for the sinuses and especially important with the challenging air environment. <br />\n </p>\n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\">\n<div id=\"file-287656\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\">\n<div class=\"content\">\n    <img class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"6\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/normalife_3_black.jpg?itok=RxjtrbyC\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1697\" alt=\"\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"image-caption\">\n<em>Illustrations by Gian Furlan </em>\n</div>\n<h2>Break my fast</h2>\n<p>On the 16th hour after my last meal, I have my most important meal of the day. I start with a large green smoothie. Then in an hour or so I will have a salad with greens, beans, olives, tomatoes, avocado and berries with lemon olive oil and sea salt.</p>\n<p>If you give this time to your well being in the morning, it makes a statement about how you care for yourself and that interprets into your self-confidence and self-esteem – and in turn folks treat you respectfully. §<br />\n </p>\n<div hues","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~3/JYZs5yGJqys/piaget-new-high-jewellery-collection-celebrates-bold-hues","description":"<p>Piaget revisits stalwart artistry techniques for the&nbsp;<em>Wings of Light </em>high <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/jewellery\" title=\"Jewellery\">jewellery</a> collection. Marquetry – where miniscule pieces of material are fitted together to create intricate new designs – becomes a pastiche of brilliantly coloured feathers embellished with sapphires and spinel for the Majestic Plumage set, pictured above. With an opulent large tourmaline stone at its centre, it makes for a striking necklace; thoughtfully designed, the plumage can also be removed and worn as an ear cuff or an earring in two parts.</p> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-287329\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"piaget watch\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"1\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/piaget-2.jpg?itok=1UhgrECq\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1400\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<div class=\"image-caption\">\n  Piaget \n <em>Wings of Light </em>Secret Cenote Cuff Watch&nbsp; \n</div> \n<p>Other pieces continue to play on the patterns in colour, with the Cenote watch injecting a more geometric rigidity into its mosaic of blues and greens. The sapphires and diamonds frame a dial in black opal, a stone which was first seen in Piaget’s designs in the Sixties. Then, they were used as an avant-garde rejection of perfect symmetry – here, the more uniform grid-like design of the whole is softened by the aquatic hues of the gems.</p> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-287330\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"piaget\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"2\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/piaget-3.jpg?itok=-zy0c2A_\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1400\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<div class=\"image-caption\">\n  An artisan works on a piece from the Piaget \n <em>Wings of Light</em> Rainbow Light set \n</div> \n<p>Sophisticated technical finishes are again at the heart of the Rainbow Light set, where gold is engraved for a textured finish, a highly delicate process due to the metal’s more pliable nature. It is juxtaposed against an intricate marquetry in leather, wood and mother-of-pearl. Shaping and positioning the mother-of-pearl so&nbsp;to ensure maximum comfort when wearing the piece proved especially testing for the artisans, who during the cutting process employed a curved stand to represent the curves of the body. §</p> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-287331\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~4/JYZs5yGJqys\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\" />","descriptionType":"text/html","publishedDate":"Sun, 23 Aug 2020 08:00:00 +0000","feedId":9788,"bgimg":"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/wp_large/s3/2020/08/piaget-feat.jpg","linkMd5":"64f17c687596288fb79720b9bc7e8e4f","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn19@2020_1/2020/08/25/00-35-15-869_164b1db05d82b15d.webp","destWidth":485,"destHeight":565,"sourceBytes":33765,"destBytes":29000,"author":"","enclosureType":"image/jpeg","enclosureUrl":"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/wp_large/s3/2020/08/piaget-feat.jpg","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/piaget-2.jpg?itok=1UhgrECq":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn90@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-19-572_1a9b1df816b3ee1f.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/piaget-3.jpg?itok=-zy0c2A_":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn4@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-16-346_6502254919efd96d.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/piaget-4.jpg?itok=XJQ5SLyU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn39@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-17-197_2b6535fbf40fff44.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~4/JYZs5yGJqys":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn44@2020_3/2020/08/25/00-35-20-518_964eae4e003db245.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598315696877},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 08:34:56","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:34:56","title":"Blaque makes space for Black people in the fitness and wellness industry","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~3/7HZCQRN7VzI/blaque-new-fitness-club","description":"<p>With <a href=\"https://www.wallpaper.com/tags/fitness\" target=\"_self\">fitness</a> and <a href=\"https://www.wallpaper.com/tags/wellness\" target=\"_self\">wellness</a> being of top priority now more than ever, the arrival of Blaque, the first luxury fitness club specifically designed to cater to the needs of Black communities, couldn’t come at a better time.</p>\n<p>Founded by T’Nisha Symone, a fitness instructor and lifestyle coach who’s had a decade’s worth of experience in the industry, Blaque is a holistic concept that will address both the physical and mental health needs of its patrons.<br />\n <br />\n‘Blaque is about making space for Black people in the fitness and wellness industry,’ says Symone, a first-generation Jamaican-American from Queens, New York. ‘That definition has evolved because of the times that we are in. Making space was extremely literal when we first started, and now it’s really about recognising that the space we haven’t had is not just about physically showing up to a club.’</p>\n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\">\n<div id=\"file-287151\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\">\n<div class=\"content\">\n    <img alt=\"man doing handstands against grey background\" title=\"man doing handstands against grey background\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"1\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/blaque_body3.jpg?itok=K322f91B\" width=\"1460\" height=\"2277\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>‘Really, when you go into a fitness space now, it’s such a focal point in people’s lives,’ she continues. ‘[It’s] where you socialise and get the resources that help you to live. Ultimately, knowing that we’re creating a space where we’re able to cater to all these unmet needs in the Black community, was why the name fit.</p>\n<p>It’s about Black people and not just fitness. The whole premise of the industry is to optimise lives and to create a space where people can live well.’<br />\n <br />\nBlaque makes the Black experience the focal point of all its services, from the classes offered to the music that is played (think: afrobeats, hip hop and compas), and the beauty and grooming products available (like whipped shea butter and Black-owned haircare brands). </p>\n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\">\n<div id=\"file-287152\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\">\n<div class=\"content\">\n    <img class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"2\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/landscape2_blaque.jpg?itok=0HYFnbi_\" width=\"1460\" height=\"895\" alt=\"\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>‘Blaque is an inclusive space for movement. As a space focused on the wellness of the Black community, it’s important to us that we consider the relatively limited experience that the fitness industry has with Black people. When class concepts are born out of Black culture (such as hip hop dance), they are repackaged to serve predominantly white members. But much of fitness culture was born out of what has been popularised in our euro-centric society,’ explains Symone. <br />\n <br />\nSymone has been refining the concept since April 2019 and was ready to sign a lease on a space the week that New York City went into lockdown. While the opening of a physical space is still very much on the cards, Symone is currently crowd-funding towards the launch of a digital platform that will host guided meditations, provide fitness coaching, nutritional coaching, and facilitate community connections, that are targeted for the Autumn.<br />\n <br />\n‘Crowd-funding is a really powerful [tool] where we can put the power into the hands of the community, rather than people who are very far removed from the ones we are trying to serve,’ explains Symone about her chosen route.</p>\n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\">\n<div id=\"file-287188\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\">\n<div class=\"content\">\n    <img alt=\"man doing downward stretch against grey background\" title=\"man doing downward stretch against grey background\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"3\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/blaque4.jpg?itok=jeru_iRb\" width=\"1460\" height=\"2190\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>‘I feel often times that we don’t have so much autonomy over the companies that come into our neighborhoods. They’re just there and we take them. I felt like this was a great opportunity for our community to essentially vote for what they want with their own dollars. It’s about a cohesive community rather than one individual or a few individuals being able to dictate the world around them.’</p>\n<p>Ultimately, Blaque is set to be a place where the physical, mental, and lifestyle needs of Black people will be catered for. ‘The fact that we could walk into service-based businesses and just expect that whatever they offered didn’t work for us, it was just how life is – I felt like that was a problem,’ Symone shares about her motivation.</p>\n<p>‘I’ve worked in the fitness industry for ten years and even the geographical separation between where I lived and where I worked was a daily reminder of the prerequisite to distance myself from my roots to make a living in the fitness industry.’ she adds.</p>\n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\">\n<div id=\"file-287193\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\">\n<div class=\"content\">\n    <img alt=\"man doing side stretch against a grey background \" title=\"man doing side stretch against a grey background \" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"4\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/blaque5_0.jpg?itok=5lsXCPYa\" width=\"1460\" height=\"2190\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>‘In order to access opportunity in the industry, I was relegated to serving a primarily white member base instead of my own community which is where the real need is. There is a wild juxtaposition between waking up at 4am to go to work in midtown Manhattan and improve the lives of people whose experiences don’t reflect yours while watching your own community’s health suffer.’</p>\n<p>And while Blaque certainly does not exclude people of other backgrounds, it is specifically designed to meet the needs of members of the Black community first. ‘There is something so unapologetic in the name, which I love, because it’s important to say who we are,’ Symone says. ‘We are very specific about who we’re serving and that’s a group of people that haven’t been served for a really long time. There’s really no shame in that.’ §</p><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~4/7HZCQRN7VzI\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"text/html","publishedDate":"Mon, 17 Aug 2020 08:00:00 +0000","feedId":9788,"bgimg":"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/wp_large/s3/2020/08/feature_blaque.jpg","linkMd5":"d1a0eaf57fe87725866877cdf17f630e","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn28@2020_6/2020/08/25/00-35-15-834_cd0691bfdb8b5759.webp","destWidth":484,"destHeight":565,"sourceBytes":28733,"destBytes":20314,"author":"","enclosureType":"image/jpeg","enclosureUrl":"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/wp_large/s3/2020/08/feature_blaque.jpg","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/blaque_body3.jpg?itok=K322f91B":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn42@2020_1/2020/08/25/00-35-18-915_66c6eccaed49f699.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/landscape2_blaque.jpg?itok=0HYFnbi_":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn67@2020_5/2020/08/25/00-35-18-066_196e09ff802d80a1.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/blaque4.jpg?itok=jeru_iRb":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn28@2020_3/2020/08/25/00-35-16-524_69781b3481a5f00a.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/blaque5_0.jpg?itok=5lsXCPYa":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn98@2020_3/2020/08/25/00-35-18-382_e186a38d9276ba91.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~4/7HZCQRN7VzI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn2@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-18-961_5a5bcb2128990a37.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598315696879},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 08:34:56","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:34:56","title":"I do! Say yes to engagement rings with an edge","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~3/N9MnMKF1aNo/say-yes-to-engagement-rings-with-an-edge","description":"<p>Lockdown, as we have learnt this year, is the ultimate test of endurance for every area in our lives: most notably, in our relationships. Many, it seems, have emerged victorious, with jewellers reporting a spike in engagement ring purchases for those who have enjoyed confinement together in close quarters. ‘We have seen an increase in sales within fine rings during lockdown and interestingly across all different price points,’ says Tanika Wisdom, <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/jewellery\" title=\"Jewellery\">jewellery</a> buyer at Matches Fashion. ‘We have seen more traction with statement styles; they all have a point of difference and stones range from diamonds to precious multi-coloured stones.’ For a ring with a difference, traditional elements such as gold and diamonds can be&nbsp;transformed with subtle design tweaks, making this most romantic of rings both special and surprising.</p> \n<h2>Nancy Newberg<br /> &nbsp;</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-287308\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"nancy newburg engagement ring\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"14\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/nancy-landy-main.jpg?itok=nM7RUBBn\" width=\"1460\" height=\"814\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Los Angeles based fine <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/jewellery\" title=\"Jewellery\">jewellery</a> designer Nancy Newberg taps into the trend with her new bridal collection,&nbsp;<em>Modern Love</em>, which unites a wealth of alternative options for those looking to avoid the more traditional. The collection mixes metals, edging gold with black and diamonds for rings that eschew sentimentality. All the new pieces cut architecturally bold silhouettes, but it is the perfect symmetry in this piece, when juxtaposed against a mash of textures, that makes it the one for us.</p> \n<h2>Katkim</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-286476\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"Katkim ring\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"13\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/floating-asscher-diamond-ring.jpg?itok=Y_4lRsSG\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1400\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Katherine Kim is the LA-based designer behind fine <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/jewellery\" title=\"Jewellery\">jewellery</a> brand Katkim. A <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/jewellery\" title=\"Jewellery\">jewellery</a> education at both Central Saint Martin’s and New York’s Fashion Institute of Technology means Kim’s style has been finely honed, and she has made a combination of fuss-free lines and surprising design tweaks her own. The Floating Asscher diamond ring marks a signature setting for her: by turning the traditional positioning quite literally on its head, she savours the elements which make an engagement ring so precious, while adding the wry humour often lacking from this most romantic of accessories.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>Maison Dauphin at Dover Street Market</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285677\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"maison dauphin ring\" title=\"maison dauphin ring\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"1\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-maison-dauphin.jpg?itok=UNCu1whe\" width=\"1460\" height=\"895\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Charlotte Dauphin de la Rochefoucauld’s eponymous <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/jewellery\" title=\"Jewellery\">jewellery</a> brand is synonymous with sculptural design. Her jewels frequently offer unexpected qualities: in this rose gold ring the off-centre placing of the diamond, when paired with the clean break of the traditional circle, presents a chic and modern engagement ring alternative.</p> \n<h2>Melissa Kaye</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285678\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"melissa kaye rings\" title=\"melissa kaye rings\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"2\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-melissa-kaye.jpg?itok=wgCKfjY7\" width=\"1460\" height=\"895\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Engagement rings don’t come much cooler than Melissa Kaye’s neon enamel collection, which intersperse traditional elements with fluorescent pops of colour. Enamel in black or white – or the more contemporary neon pink or yellow – gets a chic rethink when paired with more conventional yellow gold and diamonds.</p> \n<h2>Shahla Karimi<br /> &nbsp;</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285679\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"shahla karma rings\" title=\"shahla karma rings\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"3\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-shahla.jpg?itok=2nJFRtvR\" width=\"1460\" height=\"896\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Shahla Karimi’s designs, handcrafted in NYC’s Diamond District, cut architecture-inspired silhouettes in recycled gold or platinum. The Mid-Century series of rings pay tribute to architects including Louis Kahn, Mies van der Rohe and Frank Lloyd Wright with plays on vertically-stacked baguettes, negatives spaces and clean aesthetics.</p> \n<h2>Le Gramme</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285680\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"le gramme ring\" title=\"le gramme ring\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"4\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-le-gramme.jpg?itok=_BR2huBD\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1401\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Le Gramme’s wedding rings, like all their pieces, embody a simple concept. Named after their weight, the emphasis is on form, function and succinct design. Originally created for men, we love the minimalist nature of this piece which would lend itself well to an engagement ring; a clandestine inner circle of diamonds a chic statement for those who see no need to make one.</p> \n<h2>Kavant &amp; Sharart</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285681\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"kavant ring\" title=\"kavant ring\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"5\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-kavant.jpg?itok=ham4RFfL\" width=\"1460\" height=\"894\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Frozen on the crest of a wave, the Talay Dancing Wave ring in brushed yellow gold and diamonds eschews sentimentality, instead capturing the drama of an engagement with sensuous and undulating curves.</p> \n<h2>Georg Jensen</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285682\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"Georg Jensen rings\" title=\"Georg Jensen rings\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"6\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-goerg-jensen.jpg?itok=E2rqJ4Go\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1399\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Georg Jensen’s sculptural silhouettes lend themselves well to engagement rings which are more elegant than elaborate. Designer Regitze Overgaard’s influence is obvious in this year’s Curve collection, which is characterised by the pure lines the Danish design house is celebrated for.</p> \n<h2>Mateo at Matches Fashion</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285683\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"mateo ring\" title=\"mateo ring\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"7\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/ring-mateo.jpg?itok=TMWaEG-Q\" width=\"1460\" height=\"895\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>At first glance a traditional emerald-cut showstopper, the Point of Focus diamond and topaz ring from Jamaican designer Matthew Harris offers up unexpected details upon a second look.</p> \n<h2>Sardo at Dover Street Market</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285684\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"sardo ring\" title=\"sardo ring\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"8\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-sardo.jpg?itok=GrK3KTOI\" width=\"1460\" height=\"895\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Fluidity lies at the core of former architecture student Elena Sardo’s pieces. Made in Italy, this Roots and Wings ring encapsulates her philosophy of lightness, with dynamic branches of white gold and diamond leaves appearing to move with the wearer.</p> \n<h2>Bucherer</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285685\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"Bucherer rings\" title=\"Bucherer rings\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"9\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-bucherer.jpg?itok=IKdfe2Hd\" width=\"1460\" height=\"895\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Fine <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/jewellery\" title=\"Jewellery\">jewellery</a> becomes fun in Bucherer’s Dizzler rings, which integrate rollers crafted from precious metal between the inner and outer rings for tactile and colourful pieces. Spinning in opposite directions, yet ultimately linked together, as an alternative engagement ring they entrench playfulness with meaning.</p> \n<h2>Shihara</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285686\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"shihara ring\" title=\"shihara ring\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"10\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-shihara-2.jpg?itok=NHXo7nsa\" width=\"1460\" height=\"894\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Shihara’s <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/jewellery\" title=\"Jewellery\">jewellery</a> is deceptively simple, keeping aesthetics to a minimum and focusing instead on clear, precise silhouettes which play with the ideas around how <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/jewellery\" title=\"Jewellery\">jewellery</a> can be worn. The Un-Signet Rough Diamond ring is designed to ensure all eight sides of the octahedral uncut rough diamond can be seen. In a romantic quirk for an engagement ring, the diamond is positioned to ensure the tip is touching the wearer’s skin at all times.</p> \n<h2>Ana Khouri</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285687\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"ana khouri ring\" title=\"ana khouri ring\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"11\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-ana-kohuri.jpg?itok=OSE1Vl8z\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1400\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Ana Khouri’s <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/jewellery\" title=\"Jewellery\">jewellery</a> twists traditional concepts: with the unexpected setting of a diamond here and a just slightly off-centre placing there, her jewels are predictable only in their unpredictability. All of the expected elements are present in the Mirian ring, but with a swirl and a flourish, they become wholly new.</p> \n<h2>Hancocks</h2> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-285688\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"hancocks ring \" title=\"hancocks ring \" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"12\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-hancocks.jpg?itok=muGSggmt\" width=\"1460\" height=\"894\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Understatement is key in Hancocks’ new collection of gypsy-set rings, so-called after they were designed specifically to fool highwaymen in the early nineteenth century as to the true value of the gemstone. The stones are inlaid to ensure they sit just below the surface; shying away from the ostentatious, they nod to the prevalent mood with no compromise on design. §</p>\n<img +0000","feedId":9788,"bgimg":"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/wp_large/s3/2020/08/nancy-feat.jpg","linkMd5":"d715606fbb4502aaf66785146d555392","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn64@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-14-831_7009087e3c8dc77a.webp","destWidth":485,"destHeight":565,"sourceBytes":14019,"destBytes":9208,"author":"","enclosureType":"image/jpeg","enclosureUrl":"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/wp_large/s3/2020/08/nancy-feat.jpg","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/nancy-landy-main.jpg?itok=nM7RUBBn":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn18@2020_5/2020/08/25/00-35-20-387_90e2088e4d2fd1e2.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/floating-asscher-diamond-ring.jpg?itok=Y_4lRsSG":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn82@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-18-280_39fdd287ca695745.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-maison-dauphin.jpg?itok=UNCu1whe":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn97@2020_6/2020/08/25/00-35-17-547_bf9ac0bd1b30058c.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-melissa-kaye.jpg?itok=wgCKfjY7":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn13@2020_4/2020/08/25/00-35-17-680_fe179c2a3d25ae01.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-shahla.jpg?itok=2nJFRtvR":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn2@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-19-647_2a8802b776d5c191.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-le-gramme.jpg?itok=_BR2huBD":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn46@2020_4/2020/08/25/00-35-19-261_debd96fd7bc6fd07.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-kavant.jpg?itok=ham4RFfL":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn32@2020_1/2020/08/25/00-35-17-164_ef4d9df5a476d115.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-goerg-jensen.jpg?itok=E2rqJ4Go":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn64@2020_1/2020/08/25/00-35-16-131_c36cf601db2e250c.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/ring-mateo.jpg?itok=TMWaEG-Q":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn32@2020_4/2020/08/25/00-35-20-949_85aa2216bfb6f8d6.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-sardo.jpg?itok=GrK3KTOI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn82@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-20-896_eeb276d0f3cbaa8e.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-bucherer.jpg?itok=IKdfe2Hd":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn30@2020_3/2020/08/25/00-35-19-249_d1aa744d4ac5bfba.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-shihara-2.jpg?itok=NHXo7nsa":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn74@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-18-207_7d9ef10b8db34bd0.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-ana-kohuri.jpg?itok=OSE1Vl8z":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn21@2020_5/2020/08/25/00-35-18-380_fec428985fbeac10.webp","https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/rings-hancocks.jpg?itok=muGSggmt":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn72@2020_2/2020/08/25/00-35-19-392_08d0495fd5139969.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~4/N9MnMKF1aNo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn58@2020_3/2020/08/25/00-35-17-218_da144869038476d7.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598315696880},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 08:34:56","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:34:56","title":"Yves Béhar-designed underwater research station is inspired by 1960s design","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~3/DUu_Vrjxt_I/yves-behar-underwater-research-station-1960s-design","description":"<p>To the unfamiliar, the world of subsea research is weighed down by an ageing image of bright yellow bathyscaphes and soggy woollen berets. Although polar regions have recently received a major fillip in design distinction, serious underwater architecture has been overlooked, with only <a href=\"https://www.wallpaper.com/travel/snohetta-under-restaurant-baly\" target=\"_self\">eyeball-snaring forays into restaurants</a> and hotels surfacing.</p> \n<p>Proteus is a new venture into design for the deep, overseen by <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/yves-behar\" title=\"Yves Béhar\">Yves Béhar</a>’s fuseproject studio for a very distinguished client, the filmmaker and ocean conservationist Fabien Cousteau, grandson of the celebrated Jacques Cousteau. A proposed HQ for the Fabien Cousteau Ocean Learning Center, Proteus is designated to sit on a plot about 18m beneath the waves just off the Caribbean island of Curaçao.</p> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-287312\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"4\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/proteus_process-sketch_002_land.jpg?itok=gLNTX3B6\" width=\"1460\" height=\"853\" alt=\"\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<div class=\"image-caption\">\n  Proteus early sketches \n</div> \n<p>The project has been a couple of years in the making. ‘Early in the project two years ago, Fabien Cousteau and I looked at many exploratory designs from the 1960s and 70s,’ Béhar explains, ‘it was a golden era of interest for the oceans pioneered by the Cousteau family history.’ The brief was to develop Proteus using new materials, especially composites, and create what Béhar calls a ‘a state-of-the-art scientific environment with a comfortable social interior space.’&nbsp;</p> \n<blockquote class=\"w-wide-quote\">\n <p> ‘I have always had a strong connection and appreciation for the ocean. There’s a respect for the ocean – its power and its mystery.’ </p>\n</blockquote> \n<p>This kind of lab is essential for long-term research, as they allow divers to become acclimatised to undersea pressures. Proteus is a modular design with space for up to 12 people at a time. ‘The technology to make Proteus a reality is here, from fabrication coming from modern hull design and the use of composite materials to sustainably powering the station with a mix of renewable sources including wind, solar and Ocean Thermal Energy Conversion (OTEC),’ Béhar explains. For Cousteau, a permanent underwater research station is a lifelong ambition, one that aligns with a lifetime of involvement with studying and conserving ocean habitats. Béhar is totally on board with the ethos. ‘As a California resident and long-time surfer, I have always had a strong connection and appreciation for the ocean. There’s a respect for the ocean – its power and its mystery.’</p> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-287289\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"1\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/proteus_full_view_0.jpg?itok=OKXdE0b1\" width=\"1460\" height=\"1030\" alt=\"\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>Ultimately, the Proteus station is projected to be around 4,000 sq ft, over three times larger than any other undersea habitat. Béhar’s early sketches show an organic circular structure, anchored to the seabed on legs, with a spiralling ramp connecting two principal cylindrical spaces. Mounted off the spiral are living and working pods, giving the facility the look of a piece of growing coral or an exotic shell. The winding ramp houses the common spaces, including the living room and galley and there’s also a moon pool, an open water dock for submersibles. Béhar is particularly proud of the inclusion of a ‘greenhouse’, a potentially vital source of fresh food for a habitat where open flames are banned. ‘The larger area is where scientists and aquanauts spend most of their indoor worktime. These are open and convivial as being underwater for weeks can be isolating,’ says Béhar, adding that the ramp is also a good spot for exercising.</p> \n<p>There are still details to finesse. ‘Most of the technology is available today, but some will have to be created as we go forward,’ says Cousteau, ‘For example, the submarine coupling needs to be determined. It’s a little like the International Space Station, when you have to couple other vessels to it. We have the same issue down below, but instead of the vacuum of space, we have to deal with the multiple atmospheres, or pressures, of water. It is also dependent on the type of sub used.’ Cinematic in scope and scale, Cousteau and Béhar are hoping that Proteus brings fresh awareness of the issues facing the ocean, as well as providing a platform for ongoing discovery. §</p> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-287294\" class=\"file file-image file-image-png\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img 08:34:56","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:34:56","title":"Melbourne’s MPavilion reflects upon its contribution to urban health","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/Wallpaperfeed/~3/uroBMUEAFxw/mpavilion-book-naomi-milgrom-foundation-australia","description":"<p>Since it’s first edition six years ago, the MPavilion has become a highly-anticipated event for the city of&nbsp;Melbourne and all architects, collaborators and visitors involved.&nbsp;An initiative of&nbsp;the Naomi Milgrom Foundation, the pavilion is hosted in&nbsp;Queen Victoria Gardens and&nbsp;designed&nbsp;by a new architect each year. It is&nbsp;a worthy example of the benefits that architecture can have on public spaces and the urban community –&nbsp;Wallpaper* has keenly followed its evolution over the years, with favourite designs including&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.wallpaper.com/architecture/mpavilion-carme-pinos-australia\">Carme Pinos’ dynamically unfolding timber canopy</a>&nbsp;and <a href=\"https://www.wallpaper.com/architecture/mpavilion-2019-glenn-murcutt-melbourne-australia\">Glenn Murcutt’s light and low-slung pavilion</a> inspired by a Balinese house.</p> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-287527\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"MPavilion book design\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"3\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/internals-mock-up-5.jpg?itok=3Q0TCp8b\" width=\"1460\" height=\"1526\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-287528\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"Book design\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"4\" src=\"https://cdn.wallpaper.com/main/styles/responsive_1460w_scale/s3/mockup.jpg?itok=SJ1hGKLK\" width=\"1460\" height=\"876\" />\n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<div class=\"image-caption\">\n  Designed&nbsp;by&nbsp;creative agency Studio Ongarato, the book features colourful, graphic illustrations and \n <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/typography\" title=\"Typography\">typography</a> \n</div> \n<p>The Naomi Milgrom Foundation has now launched a new book to chart&nbsp;the success of the MPavilion – bringing together stories about its social impact through images and essays by architects and writers. The MPavilion is a core part of the foundation’s mission: enriching Australian cultural life by engaging new audiences with&nbsp;exceptional art, design and architecture and exploring the social, economic and environmental value of architecture.</p> \n<p>Featuring contributions from each of the MPavilion architects from 2014 to 2019 –&nbsp;Sean Godsell, Amanda Levete, Bijoy Jain, <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/tags/rem-koolhaas\" title=\"Rem Koolhaas\">Rem Koolhaas</a>, David Gianotten, Carme Pinós, and Glenn Murcutt – the book also celebrates the collaborators behind the scenes and what goes into the&nbsp;building of an iconic city pavilion.</p> \n<div class=\"media-element-container media-wysiwyg\"> \n <div id=\"file-287529\" class=\"file file-image file-image-jpeg\"> \n  <div class=\"content\"> \n   <img alt=\"Amanda Levete MPavilion\" class=\"media-element file-wysiwyg\" data-delta=\"5\"
